Japanese Fishing Boat in Distress Towed Back to Sasebo Port 44

More Than One Hundred Crew Members, Three Rescued

The Naval Ministry Attaches Great Importance

A Committee Has Been Formed to Investigate

Nagasaki - The ill-fated torpedo boat Tomozuru was towed by the warship Tatsuta to Kawaharapu in Sasebo Port at 7:00 AM this morning, and the ship's hull was immediately broken open to retrieve corpses. Last night at midnight, people inside the boat were still responding, but this morning there was no sound. There were a total of 113 people on board the boat, and their survival is unknown. Two naval warships and four naval aircraft are searching the sea. About 1,000 family members and relatives arrived in Sasebo this morning to visit their loved ones. The train station was very chaotic. (China United Press, 13th)

Nagasaki - After the Tomozuru was towed to Tawarapu, workers were hammering on the outside of the ironclad when there was a response from inside. The ship's hull was broken open, and when a light was shone inside, three engine crew members crawled out and were immediately sent to the naval hospital for treatment. According to them, there are still eight survivors. Efforts are being made to enter and rescue them. The ships and planes searching for corpses at sea have not yet found a body. (China United Press, 13th)

Sasebo - The ill-fated Tomozuru was an unrestricted warship of the First Replenishment Plan. It was completed in Maizuru Port on February 23rd of this year at a total cost of 2 million yen and a displacement of 527 tons. It is the newest type of torpedo boat. The Second Replenishment Plan is currently under consideration in the Diet. (Dentsu News Agency, 13th)

Efforts to Rescue 45

Sasebo - The Naval Ministry announced that the ill-fated Tomozuru was towed by the Tatsuta to Tawarapu near Anosaki outside Sasebo Port at 7:00 AM this morning. It is avoiding wind and waves there and starting to rescue the crew members. On the other hand, the ships and flying boats attached to the Sasebo Garrison Squadron have been dispatched to search for crew members on the sea and coast outside the port. At 12:45 PM, it was discovered that there were survivors in the rear of the Tomozuru. The rescue team bravely transported air into the boat, placed electric lights in the water, and transported milk and other food. At 3:05 PM, three engine crew members were rescued from the rear. The three engine crew members who were rescued from the brink of death are in good spirits, so there may be more survivors to be rescued. The entire rescue is expected to be completed around 10:00 PM. Currently, the Tomozuru in Tawarapu has four floating barrels tied to both sides to increase buoyancy. On one side, the hull of the boat is being hollowed out to try to rescue from there. According to a crew member of the Tatsuta, the ship that towed the Tomozuru, the red hull of the Tomozuru was facing the sky, and while drifting, two crew members jumped out, intending to be rescued, but they were both washed into the sea by the waves and disappeared. At that time, due to fog, waves, and wind, the Tomozuru was towed at a speed of only one knot. The sound of people inside the Tomozuru knocking was unbearable. (Dentsu News Agency, 13th)

Eyewitness Account of the Accident 46

Sasebo - Lieutenant Commander Okabe, the deputy commander of the torpedo boat Chidori, which participated in the exercise at the same time as the Tomozuru, talked about the situation at the time of the Tomozuru's accident, saying that the flagship Tatsuta, Chidori, and Tomozuru set out from the Sasebo Port outer island waterway at 1:00 AM on the 12th. Upon receiving the order from Rear Admiral Suzuki, the garrison commander, they immediately began the exercise of attacking the Tatsuta. At that time, the Chidori led the formation, followed by the Tomozuru. The Manazuru did not participate in the exercise due to engine failure. The Chidori and Tomozuru sandwiched the Tatsuta in the middle and pursued towards Shishiki Island. At that time, the wind and waves were very strong, and seawater was constantly washing the deck. The ship's body tilted very sharply, and objects inside the ship fell one after another. The exercise ended at 4:30 AM. At this time, the Tomozuru's firing signal suddenly disappeared, and it was known that it was missing. The Chidori and the flagship Tatsuta worked together to search for its whereabouts. (Japan United Press, 13th)

The Naval Ministry Attaches Great Importance 47

(Tokyo) - The Naval Ministry attaches great importance to the accident of the torpedo boat Tomozuru. The Tomozuru is a new and sophisticated boat that the Navy boasted about. The accident occurred three days after its completion, which is considered a serious problem. This is of concern to the Japanese naval authority, and it is feared that it will affect the morale of the navy. An investigation committee has been formed today, with General Nomura as the chairman. It has been decided to go to Sasebo tomorrow morning to urge the committee members to investigate the cause of the accident. Colonel Sakon, the second director of the Naval General Staff, departed at 9:43 PM tonight. Construction technology officials from Kure, Yokosuka, and other important ports are also heading to Sasebo one after another. (China United Press, 13th)

Emergency Questions in the Lower House 48

(Tokyo) - The House of Representatives convened at 1:00 PM today. Naval Minister Osumi made a temporary request to speak and reported the course of the torpedo boat Tomozuru's accident. He said that the cause of the incident has not yet been determined. After the warship "Hayasui" encountered an accident in the past, the naval authorities studied shipbuilding technology and implemented countermeasures for various tasks. However, this time another incident occurred, which is very regrettable. In view of this incident, the authorities will take necessary countermeasures to ensure that no such incidents occur in the future.

Uchida Shinya of the Seiyukai party raised an emergency question about this. The Tomozuru is one of the First Replenishment Plan, and it has only been a few days since its launch. It is regrettable to hear this report. According to reports, the waves were three meters high at the time of the Tomozuru's accident. Such waves are not uncommon. It is a disgrace for Japan's proudest new warship to have an accident at the entrance of a naval port, which makes the people doubt the concept of national defense. Regarding the issue of building sixteen torpedo boats of 600 tons or less in the Second Replenishment Plan, I once advised Naval Minister Osumi on their performance. However, the authorities plan to complete them before 1937, when the London Naval Treaty expires. What is the reason for this? Does the naval authority still intend to continue building the sixteen torpedo boats in this Second Replenishment Plan?

Naval Minister Osumi replied that the naval authorities have now decided to organize an investigation committee with the greatest authority to investigate the cause. The Naval Minister then reported the news that three crew members of the Tomozuru had been rescued. The entire assembly applauded to express their gratitude. (Japan United Press, 13th)

Major Personnel Who Perished 49

Sasebo - The crew of the fish boat Tomozuru totaled 113 people. The names of the main officers are as follows: Commander Lieutenant Commander Okishi Iwase, Lieutenant Chikanori Yoshimura, Lieutenant of Engineering Mantaro Yoshitani, Special Ensign Kijuro Yoshitake, Special Ensign of Engineering Kihei Oshima, Chief Petty Officer Rokuro Yasuhiro, Chief Petty Officer of Engineering Chotaro Nagano. The crew members are all from the prefectures of Shikoku and Kyushu. (Japan United Press, 13th)

Mediation Between Bolivia and Paraguay Fails 50

The League of Nations Committee Returns Home

Buenos Aires, Argentina - The League of Nations Committee, which planned to mediate the peace between Bolivia and Paraguay, is scheduled to return home on Thursday because the plan to seek indirect negotiations between the two countries has failed. The war between Bolivia and Paraguay has lasted for more than two years, and what they are fighting for is the Gran Chaco forest land. (Reuters, 12th)

Bloody Tragedy in Cuban General Strike 51

Havana - A group of strikers attacked longshoremen who "opposed the strike" today. Soldiers and marines opened fire on them, and the first bloody tragedy occurred in the Cuban general strike. As a result, a total of three people were injured and one person died. It is said that the order to open fire was indirectly issued by President Madieta. The President ordered the workers to resume work and resolve the situation peacefully. The President declared that he did not want to see the Cuban people shed blood, but to restore commercial prosperity, bloodshed was inevitable. The President continued that the Republic of Cuba is above all else. In this incident, the President believed that the government expressed sympathy for those who "opposed the strike" and stated that the Navy and Marine Corps had been ordered to prepare for incidents and provide adequate protection for workers who "opposed the strike." (National News Agency, 12th)

Bizarre Phenomena of Shouting and Cursing in the U.S. House of Representatives 52

Democratic Representatives Rebel and Pass the Pension Bill

(Washington) - When the House of Representatives violated President Roosevelt's wishes and passed the proposal to pay wartime pensions to veterans, a scene of shouting and commotion occurred. Representatives stood on the filing tables, shouting loudly and slandering each other. The government's failure was due to the rebellion of a majority of Democratic representatives. The Democratic leaders were shocked, but they expected that the bill might not be passed in the Senate. Even if the Senate passes it, President Roosevelt will veto it. It is also doubtful whether Congress will be able to override the President's veto with a two-thirds majority in the future. (Reuters, 13th)

U.S. Silver Bill 72

Senator Wheeler's Compromise Plan

(Washington) - Senator Wheeler today presented his so-called compromise plan, which would authorize the government to purchase 50 million ounces of silver per month until the gold-silver ratio of 16 to 1 is reached. (Reuters, 12th)

Reasons for Firm Silver Prices 73

(London) - The financial community believes that the continued firmness of the silver market is not due to special demand, but to the reluctance of those who have silver in hand to sell it. News from the United States indicates that President Roosevelt is bound to expand his plan and purchase large quantities of silver, because the purchase of gold has failed to achieve its goal of raising prices. No one knows whether this statement is reliable. However, American speculators have taken in approximately 200 million ounces of silver, and they will eventually have to sell it. (Reuters, 12th)

London Special Dispatch 74

Market prices are not expected to rise immediately, but they are also not expected to fall sharply, because the U.S. National Recovery Administration may not adopt plans that do not impede the real progress of the business. In general, as long as business activities arising from private consumption do not increase as much as they currently do, the U.S. authorities will not allow their efforts to reform to hinder the recovery. Therefore, in the coming months, it is advisable to continue to hold a bullish attitude towards market prices, especially for public bonds.

New Life Movement Mass Meeting of Citizens in Jiangxi Province 96

Over 100,000 People from All Walks of Life Participate

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Delivers Admonitory Speech

Nanchang Correspondence: The New Life Movement mass meeting of citizens was held at the Public Stadium at 12:00 noon yesterday (11th). The weather that day was overcast, alternating between cloudy and rainy, but the participation of various agencies, organizations, schools, and citizens was still very enthusiastic. After 9:00 a.m., people entered the venue in an orderly stream, reaching a total of over 100,000. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and his wife, Soong Mei-ling, as well as Xiong Shihui and others, also attended the meeting. The following is a detailed account of the opening ceremony and parade.

Venue Arrangement 97

The venue was set up at the Public Stadium. At the first entrance, a paifang [archway] was erected, with a bamboo cloth flag hanging above it, bearing the words "Citizens' Mass Meeting." To the left of the entrance was the broadcasting station and registration area, and in the middle left were the command platform and hygiene tent. The platform was set up to the right of the entrance, with the Party and national flags and Sun Yat-sen's portrait hanging above it. On both sides were the guest seats. In front of the platform (equipped with loudspeakers) was the chairman's seat, and on both sides were the recording seats. Two music stages were set up on both sides of the platform. The rest of the area was the standing locations for various agencies, organizations, and schools. In the center of the venue, a long wooden pole was erected as the flag-raising point. Each hygiene, speech, command, and chairman's platform was equipped with a radio receiver, so that the entire venue could hear the speeches on the platform.

Nanchang Citizens Attending the New Life Movement Mass Meeting

Proceedings of the Meeting 98

From 9:00 a.m., various agencies, organizations, schools, and citizens entered the venue in succession. At 12:30 p.m., the meeting was declared open. Xiong Shihui presided over the meeting. After the flag was raised, everyone paid respects to the flag. The chairman then led the audience in performing the rituals, after which he reported the purpose of the meeting. Before long, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and his wife, Soong Mei-ling, arrived at the meeting, and everyone in attendance took off their hats to salute. Chiang frequently nodded in response. Xiong continued with his report. Then, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek gave an admonitory speech, followed by a speech by Cheng Shih-kuei, representative of the New Life Movement Promotion Association. Deng Wenyi recited the New Life Guidelines. Finally, slogans were shouted, a parade was held, and the meeting was adjourned.

Xiong's Report 99

Comrades of the New Life Movement, today everyone has enthusiastically come to participate in this meeting despite the wind and rain. This spirit is commendable. Judging from this spirit and atmosphere of today's meeting, we can be fortunate for the success of the New Life Movement and, at the same time, even more fortunate for the prospects of the revival of the Chinese nation. The significance of today's New Life Movement mass meeting is very important. It not only requires everyone, regardless of farmers, workers, merchants, students, soldiers, men, women, old, or young, to participate, but also requires everyone, men and women alike, to implement it. In the past, the lives of the Chinese people were old-fashioned, out of step with the times, and incompatible with public and collective life. From today onward, everyone must change their past old lives into new lives. Only the discipline of a new life is in line with the times and with public and collective life. There is an old Chinese saying that goes, "Each person sweeps the snow from their own doorstep and doesn't care about the frost on their neighbor's roof." Now, the slogan of our new life must change to each person not only sweeping the snow from their own doorstep but also sweeping the frost from their neighbor's roof. Our supreme leader, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, has slightly indicated to us that "the New Life Movement, based on the principles of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, and the new life implemented through propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, is the foundation for the resurrection of the Chinese nation." From this, we can know the importance of the significance of the New Life Movement. Regarding the principles of the New Life Movement, there are three in total. If we act according to these principles, the New Life Movement can be successful. What are these three principles? In terms of time, the first is to think in your heart, the second is to write with your hand, and the third is to put it into practice with your body. The time for the first and second – thinking, writing, and speaking – has passed. From now on, everything depends on the effort of doing. As time is like this, so is space. First, our leader decides the methods; second, the staff plans the projects; and third, everyone must do it. Now, the leader's decision on methods and the staff's planning of strategies have also passed from today, and what follows is for each of us to do. We must understand that the New Life Movement is a mass and universal matter. It won't work if we rely on my leader alone, and it won't work if we rely on a small number of leaders. Only when everyone does it can it be successful. The New Life Movement is the foundation for transforming the national life, saving the country from danger, transforming society, and transforming occupations, etc. I hope everyone has a deep understanding and works hard to do it. This is the significance of today's meeting.

Chiang's Admonitory Speech 100

Compatriots of Nanchang from all walks of life, today everyone is holding the New Life Movement here. Judging from the spirit and order of this movement today, the people of Nanchang can be a model for the Chinese nation, and the people of Nanchang can be the foundation for the revival of the Chinese nation. This Chairman feels very honored and satisfied to participate in it together with all of you. We must know why the Chinese are subjected to foreign aggression and why they are looked down upon by foreigners. Here, we should think about whether the physique of us Chinese is stronger than that of foreigners. Furthermore, we should ask whether the learning and behavior of us Chinese are as disciplined as those of foreigners. Comparing the families, schools, and societies of us Chinese with those of foreigners, are they as clean and tidy as those of foreigners? Other things like eating, dressing, and walking, can we be as orderly and disciplined as foreigners? These various aspects of daily life, foreigners can do, but we Chinese cannot do them all. Therefore, the lack of discipline and the lack of cleanliness and tidiness in life affect the lack of physical strength. When foreigners come to China at any time, the Chinese do not have the strength to resist. This is the reason why the Chinese are subjected to foreign aggression and looked down upon by foreigners. In other words, the Chinese do not know how to cherish their bodies and protect their bodies. If they do not even know how to cherish their bodies, how can they love the country and protect the country? Today, the purpose of the New Life Movement, first, is to make everyone a strong citizen. If we want the country to be strong, the citizens must have strong bodies, then there will be great power, and they will have the power to protect themselves, and then they will have the power to protect the country. This way, they will not be bullied by foreigners. Compatriots of Nanchang, especially young students, should know that if you want to love the country, you must first protect your bodies. How can we protect our bodies? We must do it according to the rules of the New Life Movement. If you cannot do it according to the rules of the New Life Movement, then you cannot protect yourself. Are those who cannot protect themselves not wronged by their parents for giving birth to this body? Moreover, people who cannot cherish their bodies are not only ruining themselves but also affecting the decline of the nation. Such citizens will only be bullied by foreigners forever and will eventually not be able to avoid becoming slaves of a subjugated country. Therefore, everyone must know that if you want to be a proper citizen who is in line with the times, you must follow the rules of the New Life Movement. The rules of the New Life Movement, such as knowing propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, abiding by the rules, and loving cleanliness, etc., are all telling everyone the principles of being a good citizen. I hope everyone can understand and can do it, be a filial son at home, a good citizen in the country, a good student in school, and a strong and excellent member of society. This is the most important significance of the New Life Movement. The life you have lived in the past is the old life. The old life is called a barbaric life by foreigners. What is a barbaric life? It is equivalent to the life of ancient times. But now the new life has begun. From today on, we know the principles of the new life and do it accordingly, and from then on it will be a civilized life. Would you rather live a barbaric life or a civilized life? I think you would definitely rather live a civilized life. In that case, you must follow the New Life method, abide by the rules, know propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, such as dressing neatly, wearing your hat properly, respecting your parents at home, and respecting your teachers at school. The Premier Sun (Yat-sen) told us that we must be loyal, filial, faithful, righteous, loving, and sincere. The New Life Movement is also following the Premier's teachings, so that everyone can be loyal to the country and to their superiors, be loving to their friends, and be filial to their parents and teachers. If you understand these and can do them, it is called a civilized life that is in line with the times. People who do not understand these principles can be said to have lived in vain. Today, compatriots from all walks of life have this spirit and order, and the spirits of our Chinese ancestors in heaven must have great hope, hoping that you will save the country and save yourselves. Compatriots, from now on, do not live a barbaric life again, you must achieve the new life. This is your work to save yourselves and save the country. In addition, there is one more thing to tell you, that is, do you know what kind of background I have? I think you know that I have been a Commander-in-Chief, and I have also been the Chairman of the National Government, and now I am also the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission. What kind of person I was before, you must not know. When I was a child, I was taught by my parents and teachers every day to sweep the floor, mop the floor, cook and wash the dishes. When eating, if a few grains of rice accidentally fell, and when dressing, if two buttons were not buttoned, I would be punished by my parents and teachers. You must know that I am also a former elementary school student. Because my parents and teachers can strictly teach me, I can receive the teachings of my parents and teachers. Everyone should understand that a person is not born to be a revolutionary leader. If you can work hard, everyone can be like me. If you can achieve this kind of life, I believe that Nanchang will be able to create a large number of great people in the future to save the country and save the people. Today, I personally set an example and teach everyone, hoping that everyone can work hard and complete the revolutionary work, and I hope that everyone will start from today.

Mrs. Chiang Kai-shek on the Podium of the Nanchang New Life Movement Civic Assembly

Masquerade Parade 101

After the meeting ended, it was already past 3 o'clock, and the teams were immediately organized for the parade. In order of sequence, first were the academic circles, then the women's circles, then the business circles, the Party and government agencies, the labor circles, the people who participated freely, and the military police last. Starting from the venue, they proceeded to Huanhu South Road, turned to Zhongshan Road, and dispersed at the entrance of Deshengmen. The military police were divided into groups to maintain order along the way, and the order was good. Men, women, old, and young stood neatly on both sides of the road, without any crowding. Moreover, the accompanying military police corrected the unkempt clothes of the audience, regardless of whether they were male or female. The masquerade propaganda teams demonstrated drunkenness and opium addiction, and the middle school students of Jiangxi Province portrayed the ghost-like appearance of opium addicts, carrying a coffin on their backs with the words "Dead but not buried" written on it, which was especially enough to make people wake up. When the parade reached the intersection of Desheng Road and Huanhu Road at 4 o'clock, Cheng Shih-kuei, Director of Education Department, immediately supervised the boy scouts of various primary schools, lined up in two rows to maintain order on the left and right sides of the road. As soon as a team arrived, he directed the team according to the distance of each team's return route and dispersed them along the Yanjiang and Shawo roads to avoid mixing before and after. After each team had dispersed, Director Cheng gathered the boy scouts of various schools again, stood in a row in front, sang the New Life Movement song aloud, then shouted slogans, played music and dispersed. Calls for Development in Sichuan Province 102

Song Ziwen Cables Liu Xiang to Form a Branch of the Economic Commission

Sichuan Province Prepares to Establish an Economic Control Commission

Chengdu Correspondence: In recent months, talk of developing Sichuan Province has been rampant. Because Sichuan Province has been known since ancient times as the "Land of Abundance" with fertile land and abundant products, if it can be operated with determination, it can easily become the foundation for a strong country in the future. Therefore, the authorities in Sichuan have long determined the three steps of suppressing bandits, rehabilitation, and development for reorganizing Sichuan. Domestic enlightened people are also paying attention to this. From the Chinese Science Society holding meetings in Sichuan to the Shanghai Journalists' Group coming to Sichuan to inspect, there is also an organization of a Sichuan Inspection Group of the Chinese Institute of Engineers. Recently, Zhang Gongquan and others from the Shanghai banking industry also plan to organize a group to come to Sichuan for inspection, preparing to make large investments. The Ministry of Industry has repeatedly sent personnel to Sichuan last year to inspect mineral and industrial enterprises, and then specially appointed Fan Chongshi as the Sichuan Oil Mine Commissioner, with Liang Qiyu, the section chief of the Mining Department of the Ministry, as his deputy. Fan and Liang have formulated an exploitation plan and submitted it to the Ministry. The Shanghai Guohuo Bank plans to invest 500,000 yuan to support this cause. Song Ziwen, Chairman of the National Economic Council, Dai Jitao, President of the Examination Yuan, and Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, are also scheduled to come to Sichuan next month to inspect industrial enterprises. Song recently sent a cable to Sichuan, instructing Liu Xiang to be responsible for preparing the Sichuan branch of the Economic Commission. Previously, an American doctor visited Liu Xiang, praised the abundance of mineral deposits in Sichuan, and volunteered to contact the Luo's Fund Committee in the United States to invest in Sichuan. Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways, also agrees to complete the Chengdu-Chongqing Railway as soon as possible, advocating the issuance of public bonds with Sichuan salt revenue as collateral to serve as a railway construction fund. It can be seen that all parties are very sympathetic to the development of Sichuan.

The Rehabilitation Supervisory Office has also convened Sichuan industrial talents several times to discuss and study the development plan for Sichuan, advocating starting with improving local products and promoting production. The recent large-scale holding of the Thirteenth Sichuan Industrial Exhibition is intended for this purpose. A notice has been issued to all county construction bureaus or section chiefs in Sichuan to attend the meeting in person, and all donations and taxes that should be paid along the way for the items to be exhibited are waived to show promotion. Moreover, the promotion of imported goods and all enemy goods is prohibited at the site. This spirit is far from what previous industrial exhibitions could compare. Recently, an industrial conference was convened, deciding to establish a local product improvement committee organized by industrial institutions and specialized talents. Once it is effective in the future, it will be reorganized into the Sichuan Provincial Economic Control Commission. The conference convened its second preparatory committee a few days ago. In addition to determining the name of the Local Product Improvement Committee, it was also decided to organize seventeen specialized committees for Liangshan paper industry, Zinei grain industry, Peng County ceramics and silk weaving industry, cotton weaving industry, dyeing industry, tea industry, and various mining industries. The Supervisory Office first telegraphed the county magistrates of Liangshan, Pengshan, Zizhong, Neijiang, and other counties to send specialized talents engaged in various special industries in their respective counties to the province within March. On the one hand, the Provincial Federation of Trade Unions and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce in this city were instructed to introduce various specialized talents. The municipal government and the Industry Department are responsible for reviewing qualifications, reporting to the Supervisory Office, and hiring them separately. Once specialized talents arrive at the Department, they will hold an inauguration conference at the same time as the Local Product Improvement Committee. It is also heard that the Supervisory Office also has a change in the education policy, and has determined to focus on vocational education and train more technical talents to promote local product enterprises. Six vocational schools will be prepared to be established in Chengdu, Chongqing, Guanxian, Xufu, and Jiading. The Sichuan University and Chongqing University will be reorganized, and the Industrial and Agricultural Colleges of Chengdu will be moved to Chongqing and merged with Chongqing University as a branch of Sichuan University, focusing on science. Sichuan University in Chengdu will focus on liberal arts. The annual funding should be at least 1.2 million yuan. (Guowenshe)

Communist Bandit Ye Jianying Disturbs Xunwu 104

[Repelled by Xie's Regiment of the Guangdong Army]

Shantou Correspondence: After Chiang Dingwen returned to Xiamen on the 3rd, he convened a bandit suppression meeting on the 5th. Those present included Wei Lihuang, Commander-in-Chief of the Front, Li Yutang, Commander of the Third Division, Fan Songfu, Commander of the Seventh Division, Li Yannian, Commander of the Fifth Division, Zhao Nan, Chief of Staff, and Lin Wensheng, Director of the Headquarters. They discussed the method of liaison between the Southeast and Northwest Route Armies. The Shantou Eastern District Pacification Conference opened on the 5th. Li Yangjing, Zhang Ruigui, Huang Renhuan, Huang Yanzhen, Huang Zhiwen, and other generals all arrived. In addition to discussing local pacification issues, the dispatch of troops to suppress bandits in Jiangxi was also discussed. After the meeting on the 8th, the division commanders and representatives of the regiments all returned to their original defenses on the upper reaches of the Han River and the border of Fujian and Jiangxi. It is heard that most of the Jiangxi bandits, due to the pressure of the Central Army in northern Fujian and eastern Jiangxi, gathered in Guangchang, Shiyu, Ruijin, and Huichang, in the mountains along the Jiangxi-Fujian border. Before dawn on the 4th, over 1,000 bandits under Ye Jianying of Huichang Junmenling invaded Qingxi Sanbiao Xu. Xie Zheng's regiment stationed in Sanbiao sent troops to intercept them and met them in battle at Longgang Yaziwu. From 10 a.m. to 3 p.m., the fighting was fierce on both sides. Xie Zheng ordered the machine gunners to charge with grenades, and the bandit front line wavered. By 5 o'clock, they were defeated and returned to Luotang. Qingxi was not occupied. The Eighth Division sent an additional Chen Fengshao regiment to guard Qingxi. Now Luotang is in the hands of the bandits. The area is close to Xunwu and only tens of miles away from the border of Wuping and Pingyuan. It is the hub of land transportation between Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi, and it is the only passage that the Guangdong Army must pass through to attack Junmenling. It is heard that the Central Government has given each route army a deadline of May 1 to recover the counties in the bandit area and pursue and suppress the bandits in order to fundamentally eliminate them. Canton-Hankou Railway: Construction to Commence Soon Between Zhuzhou and Leiyang Through Public Bidding 105

Survey Team Has Reached Leiyang

Guangdong-Hunan Border Line to be Constructed

Hengyang Communication: The Canton-Hankou Railway's southern section from Hengzhou had previously been surveyed by the railway's engineering bureau, which dispatched the fifth and sixth surveying teams to carry out the measurement. They have now reached the Leiyang county border. Once the route between the Mi and Lei rivers is surveyed within the next two to three months, the entire section from Zhuzhou to Gongpingxu south of Leiyang, approximately 230 kilometers, can be put out for public bidding and construction can commence. As for the section north of Dashimen in Guangdong, crossing the provincial border and reaching Baishidu in Hunan, it has been approved by the Ministry of Railways for immediate construction. The terrain from Baishidu to Chenzhou is more complex, requiring careful comparison of various routes before a final decision can be made. Furthermore, to facilitate experienced contractors from other locations to bid on the railway, the railway engineering bureau has agreed with the Ping-Han Railway Bureau to charge workers transported by contractors at one-quarter of the ticket price, in addition to the existing free transportation of workers by the Canton-Hankou Southern Section Administration in Guangdong. The Hunan-Hubei Railway Bureau will allow free accounting. This will not only encourage more contractors to bid but also reduce the cost of road construction. (March 7th)

Songjiang 106

Meeting Convened for District Reorganization

The county government previously received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs, stating that local autonomy in this province has been implemented since the spring of the eighteenth year [of the Republic, i.e., 1929], and it has been five years with no significant achievements. While the reasons are not uniform, the excessively detailed division of local autonomy regions, causing difficulties in both talent and economy, is the most important reason. After discussion at the internal affairs meeting of the Ministry of Interior, a method for re-division was adopted, seeking convenience and submitted to the provincial government for approval and notification to all counties for compliance. According to the regulations, counties with an area of less than 2,000 square miles should not have more than eight districts. County Magistrate Jin, acting on this principle, scheduled a meeting for re-division today (14th). In addition to the district chiefs, the director of the property management office, the chief of the county government's secretariat, and members of the Party branch were all present.

Suzhou 107

Plans to Widen East, West, and Central Market Streets

The east, west, and central market streets inside Chang Gate are busy areas in Suzhou City. Banks and money shops are densely packed. The Wuxian Construction Bureau is actively planning to widen these two streets and has completed the planning. Yesterday, it was submitted to the Construction Department for review and approval. However, the Chang Gate city gate will no longer be suitable after the widening of the streets, so a decision has been made to rebuild it, and it is currently being designed.

Wuxi 108

Measures to Ban Subletting of Silk Factories

Before the sixteenth year of the Republic [i.e., 1927], there were only eighteen silk factories in Wuxi County. After the sixteenth year, more factories were added, totaling forty-nine. However, most of the added factories sublet the factories and collect interest. Each silk reeling machine requires a deposit of approximately twenty silver taels, and the monthly rent is approximately three taels and five qian. Some speculators took advantage of this opportunity to deceive farmers into borrowing money and opening factories. Unexpectedly, the silk market collapsed, resulting in heavy losses and successive closures. Disputes such as those involving the Huisheng, Qingfeng, and Taixin factories have not yet been resolved. For the sake of rectification, the county government has drafted seven provisional measures to ban subletting silk factories and submitted them to the provincial government for review and implementation. The measures are as follows: (1) These measures apply to all silk factories that rent factories for business within Wuxi County. (2) Before signing a lease, any person who rents a factory for business shall first submit in writing the names of the operating shareholders and managers, the total amount of capital, and the name, number of machines, and location of the silk factory to be rented to the Silk Factory Guild. The guild shall send personnel to verify the capital and report to the county government for record before signing the contract with the factory owner. (3) The total capital mentioned in the preceding article shall be at least one hundred silver dollars per silk reeling machine. (4) Any person who rents a factory for business shall deposit the wages guarantee deposit for female workers in a bank after signing the lease and submit the deposit book to the Silk Factory Guild before starting business. The guarantee deposit is temporarily set at twenty silver dollars per silk reeling machine, and more will be added proportionally. (5) After receiving the guarantee deposit book, the Silk Factory Guild shall issue a receipt and report it to the county government for record. (6) When a rented silk factory declares closure, if there is no outstanding wage payment, the Silk Factory Guild shall return the guarantee deposit book based on the actual closure and report it to the county government for record. (7) Violators of the provisions of Articles 2 and 3 shall be ordered to suspend business upon investigation.

Navigation Administration Orders Licheng to Suspend Navigation 109

The Shanghai Navigation Administration of the Ministry of Communications received a report from Xi Zhiqing, Zhang Jun, and other citizens of Zhouzhuang Town, Jiangyin, stating that the Xinlijiang, Lida, Feifeng, and other small steamships owned by the Licheng Shipping Bureau of Wuxi have not been repaired for many years and are very dangerous when operating on inland rivers. After receiving the report, Director Peng checked the small steamship measurement inspection and registration certificate regulations. Article 21 stipulates that the navigation period for inspected and qualified small steamships shall not exceed one year and shall not be allowed to navigate after the expiration date without re-inspection. The Xinlijiang and other small steamships have exceeded the time limit without repair, which violates the regulations. Yesterday, he sent an official letter to the county government requesting an immediate investigation to determine whether they are navigating. If they are navigating, they should be ordered to apply to the bureau for inspection. Otherwise, they should be ordered to suspend navigation to uphold the law.

Changshu 110

Robbery of Four Households in Hudian, Lakeside

Xiaohudian, located only two miles outside the southwest gate of Changshu, is home to a private shaman named Shen Wangshi, who enjoys considerable fame and a decent life. Because she is known as "Shen the Immortal," Shen also considers herself an immortal. Her family has accumulated considerable wealth and fears being coveted by bandits. In the eastern corner of her house, she built a single-eyed stove to secretly hide gold and silver jewelry and silver dollars inside. It was usually peaceful, but the location is close to the shore of Shang Lake. Suddenly, on the night of the tenth, a group of twenty to thirty bandits came from the lake and swarmed into Shen the Immortal's house. They stripped Shen of her clothes, tied her with hemp ropes, poured gasoline on her breasts, and burned her, forcing her to reveal the location of the hidden silver. Shen initially refused to confess, but after being unable to endure the pain, she told the bandits. The bandits then dug up the single-eyed stove and found more than a thousand yuan in banknotes and silver, ten gold rings, five pairs of gold bracelets, two gold pendants, a pair of gold bracelets, silver ornaments, and clothing, totaling approximately four to five thousand yuan. After the robbery, they also robbed neighboring homes, affecting four households. Fortunately, the losses were minor. Shen was also shot once during the robbery, with the bullet entering her buttocks. She is currently receiving treatment in the hospital, but Shen is nearly seventy years old and has suffered greatly, so her life is in danger. The Public Security Bureau has received the news and has sent personnel to the countryside to investigate.

Changzhou 111

Three New Banks Begin Operations

The Wujin, Xinfu, and Guohua banks, newly established in Wuyi, have been preparing for a long time. The Wujin Bank was established by local people with shares, and the president is Liu Yaoxing. It has already started operations. The Changzhou branch of the Xinfu Bank is scheduled to open on the 17th of this month, and the president is Wang Jianchang. The Changzhou branch of the Guohua Bank is scheduled to open on the 26th of this month, but will start operations on the 16th, and the president is Gu Shouxuan. Since the total collapse of the money shops, they have been replaced by banks, and there is hope for revitalization in the market.

Haimen 113

Large Group of Bandits Rob and Injure People

Xu Daiming, a resident of Xidaiming in the southwest of Daxing Town, Second District, is engaged in farming and reading and has a wealthy family, which has attracted the attention of bandits. On the midnight of the tenth, more than twenty bandits speaking local dialects suddenly came, carrying box guns, rifles, and shotguns, and rushed into the house. They went directly to Xu's bedroom, dragged Xu out of the bed, beat him with fists and feet, and forced him to hand over silver dollars. When he refused, they beat Xu's wife with a bench, causing serious injuries to both. The bandits then searched the house at will and left after about an hour. Upon inspection, the losses were estimated at more than one hundred yuan in banknotes, clothes, and ornaments. Yesterday, it was reported to the county government, requesting an investigation.

As for the court, it has interrogated Qian Wenbin, the police chief in custody for the incident, and has verified the death and injuries separately. It will send a letter to the Public Security Bureau to hand over the shooters for investigation.

Local News

Discovery of Smuggling of Chinese and Puppet Manchukuo Mail in Postal Service 115

Involved Shanghai-Dalian Trading Company

Enticing Retired Chinese Postal Workers

Xinsheng News Agency reports: Recently, Chinese postal authorities suddenly discovered that a Japanese organization called the "Shanghai-Dalian Trading Company" was colluding with retired postal workers to transport mail between China and Puppet Manchukuo. The representative of the company is Mr. Ohara. Xinsheng News Agency has obtained two confidential letters issued by the company regarding this case, which appear to be addressed to postal personnel, as well as a copy of the mailing procedure, translated and published below. It is hoped that the Chinese postal authorities will conduct a thorough investigation and crackdown.

Two Confidential Letters 116

(1) Dear Sir, After four months of satisfactory work, we were appointed by one of our Japanese staff in the Dalian Post Office to serve as steamboat postal workers, and instructed us to secretly mail the mail directly to designated institutions through the high seas. Your mail is also entrusted to us. In this way, the confidential mail will be connected to the Dalian First Railway and arrive without being delayed by the organization's sorting. It is not necessary to replace our registered receipt with a Dalian Post Office receipt, because we can now issue a Dalian receipt when we receive it. Your faithful representative, Ohara, January 26, 1934. Please send letters to P.O. Box No. 3125. (2) Dear Sir, The delays in receiving mail to Europe caused by sending mail through the Siberian local post office, resulting in delays in receiving mail from Siberia to Europe, have caused you discomfort. The establishment of this trading company can alleviate this. Mail to Europe is now sent via the Suez Canal and takes approximately thirty-five to forty-two days to arrive. As for Siberia, it only takes seventeen to nineteen days. This company is composed of three

postal commissioners and four representatives. The representatives recently retired from the postal service because they have completed their thirty-year terms. Every ship of the Dalian Steamship Company has one of our staff members from here to Dalian. We ask you to do a secret job, which is to take your mail from Shanghai to Dalian and then mail it there for further mailing via Siberia. Entrusting our postal service will be in private contact with us. We will handle it in a way that does not conflict with international postal treaties, so your mail is fully guaranteed. You can also register your mail, and when the responsible personnel return from Dalian, they can exchange the Dalian Post Office receipt for the registered receipt we issued. Chinese stamps and tariffs will be added to your mail because they respect the sovereignty and monopoly of the country's postal service. This was recognized by all members at the International Postal Conference held in London in 1929, and Dalian is also one of the members. This is a secret matter, which was banned by the Nanjing government after the Manchurian Incident. We sincerely request you to keep the secrets of this organization because, in case the post office finds out, this agency will have to close immediately. If you are unwilling to do so, please burn this letter. (Signed the same as the previous letter)

Mailing Procedure 117

(1) Please prepare your mail the day before the steamer sails, and please do not add any stamps, just like we are going to do. (2) The day before the ship sails, our representative will go to inform you, calculate the number of pieces, issue a registered receipt, and estimate the postage, and bring those mails to this agency to pay the fees and send them out. (3) At the end of each month, or after you receive the reply, we will do a collection and sorting job. If you still need a better guarantee, we can also give you a responsible senior postal worker in the Shanghai Post Office General Bureau. (4) Our reward is ten cents per piece, regardless of its weight and size. The total number of mails we send each time is limited to three full mailbags, so we sincerely ask you whether you are willing to participate in this opportunity. Please give us a reply. If the answer is negative, we can still find someone else. We are honored to be your faithful servant. Shanghai Dalian Trading Company, signed by representative Ohara.

Workers of the American-Asian Factory Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday 120

Hired Cars in the Evening to Transport Them Back to the Factory

Dagong News Agency reports: All the workers of the American-Asian Silk Weaving Factory had a dispute over the factory's reduction of wages. At around 5:00 a.m. yesterday morning, they set off in batches, gathered at the May 30th Cemetery in Zhabei, and walked together to the municipal government in the downtown area to petition. They did not arrive at the municipal government in succession until 12:00 noon. The entire police force of the seventh district and first sub-office was armed and on guard.

Municipal Government Response: After the workers arrived at the municipal government, they elected ten representatives, including Huang Baofu, Feng Xianchun, Lü Haiquan, Xia Zhiwei, Zhu Linchai, Cai Hangsong, He Yayun, Weng Bingyan, Liu Yanqing, and Pan Yuancai, to enter and petition. All the workers gathered in the square in front of the municipal government to wait. The municipal government sent Yuan Xinglu from the second section to receive them. The representatives handed over the petition and reported the details of the dispute and the details of the workers being arrested and beaten by the French patrol, requesting that a protest be filed with the French authorities and that the factory be ordered to withdraw the order to reduce wages. Mr. Yuan replied, (1) Regarding the incident of workers being beaten, it is a matter of criminal law and can be sued in court. (2) Labor-management disputes will be investigated and mediated by the Municipal Government's order to the Social Affairs Bureau. The representatives expressed their dissatisfaction and insisted that the municipal government must file a protest with the French authorities. Mr. Yuan finally instructed the workers to report the details of the conflict in detail and then verify it.

Dispersed Late: The representatives withdrew to report the answers to the workers, who expressed their dissatisfaction and stood still. After repeated persuasion by the municipal government, the workers still refused to leave, insisting that the municipal government must have a definite and satisfactory answer. The situation was quite serious for a while, and it had not dispersed until 6:00 p.m. After hearing the news, the General Labor Union immediately sent Yu Yaoqiu to rush over and persuade them again and hired many moving cars to transport the workers back to the factory in batches. It was not until about 8:00 p.m. that the transport was completed.

Some Members of the Business Community's Investigation Team to Shandong Have Returned to Shanghai 121

Some members of the Shanghai business community's investigation team to Shandong, including Wu YunChu, Hu Xiyuan, and Xu Zhiyi, returned to Shanghai by the Shanghai-Ping Express train the night before last. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the Central News Agency met with Mr. Wu YunChu, who reported the following gains from the trip. Mr. Wu first said that he and others were warmly received by all sectors in Shandong, for which he was very grateful. As for the investigation, it was only a rough idea due to the limited time. Shandong's industry and politics are gradually on track, so there is progress every day. This time, I saw that the electrical industry along the Tianjin-Pukou Railway is very developed. However, Yanzhou is slightly blocked. As for the flour mills, they are very developed because it is a producing area and the residents eat wheat. Chairman Han is now working hard to connect the hydraulic engineering project of Xiaoqing River's Wuliu Gate. After the completion, it will greatly benefit the local people because it can make the river water flow directly into the sea. Finally, he said that he regretted that he was unable to investigate in detail due to his busy schedule. The reporter asked what plans there were for the future. He replied that in April, the team still planned to go to Sichuan Province because Chairman Liu had sent several telegrams inviting them, and so on.

I am grateful to you. Respectfully, the Special District Office of the Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Guild, March 13th.

Appeal from Sugar Merchants for the Confiscation Case of Native Sugar in Beihai 125

Total Stoppage of Southern China's Native White Sugar Shipment to Shanghai

Pang Songhui Submits Additional Justification Again

Native sugar from various places such as Qiongyai, Qinlian, and other regions in Guangdong, being shipped to Shanghai, has been repeatedly fined and confiscated by the Jianghai Customs last year. Chambers of commerce and sugar merchants from those areas have sent representatives to Beijing to petition for relief. After months of investigation by the government, the truth has been clarified. The Executive Yuan issued Instruction No. 1156 at the beginning of this month, approving the Ministry of Finance to instruct for a correction of the sugar testing standards and to confirm the inspection rights at the port of export. The part regarding the reversal of old cases is still under review. However, on January 23rd of this year, 92 bags of native white sugar belonging to the Beihai sugar merchant Henghelong were detained by the Jianghai Customs in the Gu Cang warehouse. Two months have passed, and they have not been released. Sugar merchants from various places are observing the situation. According to statistics, only over 300 bags of native white sugar from Southern China have arrived in Shanghai this year, compared to over 10,000 bags in the same period last year, a world of difference. Currently, it is the peak season for native white sugar production. Sugar workshops and farmers in various places have produced white sugar, piling up like mountains. Sugar merchants dare not transport it, and they are in dire straits. Pang Songhui, the representative of the petitioners, has drafted an additional justification and reiterated the previous request to the Customs Administration. The original text is excerpted as follows: For the case of the Jianghai Customs detaining native sugar from Beihai and forcibly confiscating it, a request for relief, supplemented with reasons, reiterating the previous request, respectfully requesting review and implementation. I, in secret investigation, on January 23rd of this year, the Qinlian sugar merchant Henghelong, transported 92 bags of K-mark native white sugar from Beihai on the Hubei steamer, to be received by Fu Tianshen in Shanghai. In the case of the confiscation by the Jianghai Customs, I have previously presented two relief methods, earnestly requesting a swift and rapid decision to be granted. A month has passed, and no instructions have been given for implementation, causing deep anxiety. Now, for the sake of the Honorable Administration to easily understand the truth and quickly resolve the matter, I especially supplement the reasons as follows: (1) From the perspective of customs administration, there is no reason for confiscation. The native sugar in this case was shipped directly from Beihai to Shanghai. Upon export, it was inspected by the Beihai Customs, confirming that it was produced by the Wulilu Lun Chang Sugar Workshop in Lingshan County and was indeed pure native sugar. It was released after paying taxes in accordance with regulations. According to export customs regulations, after the goods have been inspected and loaded onto the ship, the exporting merchant has no way to interfere. When the original shipment arrives at the destination, the importing merchant declares it for import. Therefore, in this case, the native sugar could not be changed or altered in any way from export in Beihai to import in Shanghai. Now, the Jianghai Customs claims that the inspection revealed more than half foreign sugar and confiscates it, which is truly perplexing. Ultimately, do the Beihai Customs and the Jianghai Customs follow the same tax system? Why is one releasing it first and the other confiscating it later? If it is because their sugar testing standards are different, they should blame themselves for the errors in their inspection policy, and they should not make sugar merchants suffer losses for following the regulations, thereby demeaning their own credibility. This is from the perspective of customs administration, where the Jianghai Customs's decision is wrong. (2) From the perspective of light measurement inspection, there is no reason for confiscation. The sole reason for the Jianghai Customs to detain and confiscate the native sugar in this case is that the inspection showed a optical rotation of 92.8 degrees, which is proof of more than 50% foreign sugar content. It is known that there are ordinary sugar and invert sugar in sugar content. Ordinary sugar rotates light to the right, while invert sugar rotates light to the left. The level of optical rotation changes with the change in sugar content. However, the change in sugar content does not have a fixed distinction based on whether it is imported or domestically produced, or whether it is machine-made or native-made. Therefore, it is absurd and groundless for the Jianghai Customs to consider sugar with a optical rotation of over 90 degrees as foreign sugar and sugar below 90 degrees as native sugar. Moreover, this standard is still based on that set three years ago, based solely on Fujian native sugar. They adhere to it for years without adapting, completely ignoring the progress of sugar production in Guangdong Province in recent years. Last year, the Central Industrial Testing Institute chemically tested Qiongzhou native sugar, with Grade C being 92 degrees and Grade B reaching 93 degrees. The error of the current standard of the Jianghai Customs has long been proven beyond doubt. Qinlian native sugar is inherently better than that of Qiongyai, but it is still being judged by old inspection methods without correction. How unfortunate is the Qinlian sugar industry? This is from the perspective of light measurement inspection, where the Jianghai Customs's decision is wrong, two. (3) From the perspective of declaring dissenting opinions, there is no reason for confiscation. It is known that among the recent confiscations of Southern China's native sugar by the Jianghai Customs, in addition to this case, there are also cases in Shantou and Haikou. Sugar merchants in other places all willingly accept the punishment and have not been heard dissenting. But why does the merchant dare not remain silent? The reason is that the government is cracking down on smuggled foreign sugar for the sake of maintaining tax revenue and for the sake of maintaining native sugar. If they can stop smuggled goods without harming the innocent, sugar merchants would be grateful beyond words and would have no reason to dissent. But who knows that the Jianghai Customs cannot distinguish right from wrong, and equate deer with horses. Because they discovered native sugar mixed with foreign sugar elsewhere, with a optical rotation exceeding 90 degrees, they also detain and confiscate the pure Qinlian native sugar exceeding 90 degrees. Those who uphold justice are still speaking out and providing relief, but how can those who are wronged remain silent? This is from the perspective of declaring dissenting opinions, which is actually a refutation of the Jianghai Customs's decision, three. (4) From the perspective of anti-smuggling punishment, there is no reason for confiscation. Our country has not yet implemented customs laws, and tax punishments are arbitrarily changed, making it difficult to obtain a fair resolution. The case of the Haikou brown sugar being fined, which is related to this case, is one example. It is known that the Haikou sugar merchant Ganrong transported 114 bags of brown sugar to Shanghai Guangyuan, which were inspected by the Jianghai Customs and deemed to be mixed with 80% foreign sugar. They only imposed a fine of 150 silver dollars and settled the supplementary tax. In this case, 92 bags of white sugar (weighing just half of the Haikou brown sugar case) were only deemed to be mixed with over 50% foreign sugar, but the entire shipment was confiscated. The circumstances of transporting native sugar for both cases are not different, but the severity of the punishment is arbitrarily reversed. From this analogy, it is not difficult to believe that the amount and existence of alleged mixed foreign sugar can also be uttered arbitrarily, shrinking or expanding according to emotions. Sugar merchants will never have a day of relief. This is from the perspective of anti-smuggling punishment, where the Jianghai Customs's decision is wrong, four. The reasons supplemented in this case are as stated above. Now, for the sake of the Honorable Administration's thorough understanding and convenient resolution, I will further clarify the cause of this case and state it as follows: Since the increase in taxes on foreign sugar, native sugar has sold well. Qinlian white sugar, due to its more refined production and cheaper raw materials, has made significant progress. Local people are celebrating this as a good phenomenon for rural revitalization. But who knows that unscrupulous merchants elsewhere, because foreign sugar taxes are heavy, smuggle to take advantage of loopholes, using counterfeit goods to confuse the truth and smuggle mixed goods to Shanghai. The Jianghai Customs has not thoroughly investigated the sugar production in various places, but only knows that the source is from Southern China, making it easy to raise suspicion in such a situation. Added to this is the fact that customs anti-smuggling would rather wrongly punish than let go. Therefore, the seemingly sunny goods face the difficulty of even Confucius being surrounded, and the same name as Zeng Shen does not prevent Zengzi from being rumored to be a murderer. The Qinlian sugar industry, in this situation where right and wrong are unclear, has repeatedly experienced detention and fines. Initially, it was due to a misunderstanding by the customs officers, enduring and bearing the injustice for a time. But unexpectedly, after months of concealment, there is still no day to see the light of day. The crux of the matter lies in the tax commissioner's stubborn preconceptions, disregarding objective facts, thinking that merchants are mostly treacherous and good sugar must be foreign sugar. How can they know that clear water and turbid water can be distinguished by comparison, and that orchids and bright pearls can be judged by re-inspection? Therefore, not hesitating to offend, I reiterate the previous request, respectfully requesting that the two relief methods presented in the previous report be carefully considered. Officials should be dispatched to the Qinlian sugar production area for a thorough on-site inspection, or the Qinlian Sugar Industry Guangyitang should be instructed to take samples of native sugar with public certification from local party and government organs and mass organizations and send them to Beijing for open comparison and re-inspection with the detained native sugar in this case. If there is evidence of tax evasion, I will gladly accept any punishment, even death by torture. Otherwise, immediately reverse the decision according to the law and establish a method to guarantee the safety of future transportation, so that sugar merchants are not constantly struggling in dire straits, then there will be boundless good fortune. I present this straightforward statement, respectfully requesting your review. Respectfully presented to Shen, the Director of the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance,

Navy Aircraft Manufacturing Plant to Expand 129

The Ninghai Ship Aircraft Can Be Completed by the End of Next Month

The Jiangfeng Aircraft Will Fly to Various Places Next Month

A Central News Agency reporter recently met with Mr. Zeng Yijing, who provided a detailed account of the current situation and future plans of the Navy Aircraft Manufacturing Plant. The details are recorded separately below:

Construction of Additional Factory Buildings to Begin Soon 130

According to Mr. Zeng, the Ministry of Navy, in view of the rapid progress of aircraft in various countries, decided to establish the Navy Aircraft Manufacturing Plant to increase the Navy's auxiliary power. Later, due to the small size of the factory buildings, funds were allocated in the autumn of 1931 to expand the plant and build a workshop in front of the existing factory buildings. By the spring of 1932, the foundation of the workshop had been completed, but the January 28th Incident broke out, and the project was suspended. Subsequently, the Ministry of Navy drafted a plan and requested the Central Government to allocate funds for expansion. The Central Government approved and allocated over 100,000 yuan for expansion, but due to the Central Government's financial difficulties, not a single cent has been received to this day. Now, with the approval of Minister Chen, the Navy has managed to save 40,000 yuan from its own budget to be used for the construction of additional factory buildings at the Navy Aircraft Manufacturing Plant. It has now been decided to build a two-story factory building on the existing foundation. The upper floor will be used as offices, and the lower floor will be used as a workshop. The new building will be 120 feet deep. The workshop on the lower floor will be divided into three rooms. The left and right sides will be wood and metal workshops, each 10 feet wide, and the middle will be an assembly workshop, 50 feet wide, which can accommodate the assembly of six aircraft simultaneously. The original factory building will be used to store aircraft. This plan was submitted to the Navy Department last Saturday and will be implemented as soon as it is officially approved. Further expansion plans, such as purchasing additional machinery, will have to wait until funding is available.

Ninghai Ship Aircraft to Be Completed by the End of the Month 131

Mr. Zeng continued, "The plant is building an aircraft for the Ninghai warship. The fuselage has been assembled, and the wing frames have also been installed. However, some parts have not yet been delivered, and the engine will also have to be installed after the fuselage is completed. Therefore, the entire project will be delayed until the end of this month or the beginning of next month. The cost of the aircraft is estimated at over 10,000 yuan. A steel-framed destroyer is also under construction and can be completed at the same time as the Ninghai aircraft."

Jiangfeng Aircraft to Fly to Various Places 132

Furthermore, the Jiangfeng aircraft, after being converted into a land-based aircraft, has undergone five test flights at the Longhua Airfield, conducting tests on high altitude, maximum speed, and normal speed, with excellent results. The aircraft is currently stored at the airfield and is scheduled to fly to Fuzhou and other places at the beginning of next month. Permission has been obtained from the Minister of the Navy. It is planned that Chen Chengqi will fly the aircraft. The first flight will be to Fujian, and the aircraft will return to Shanghai the next day. The second flight will be to Shantou and Guangzhou, and then to Hankou, Tianjin, and other places. This is intended to promote the achievements of our country's domestically produced aircraft and to practice flying skills and familiarize oneself with domestic air routes.
